FNV PBR CLOSE TERRAIN PASS-ENTRY RUNTIME CONTRACT

Questions:
1. Which pass-entry rows does vanilla build for close terrain and adjacent land helpers?
2. Which BA9EE0 param_3 row IDs map to material arrays, zero-resource land/spec rows, and LandO/light rows?
3. What exactly is stored in entry +0x09/+0x0A arg counts, +0x0B layer byte, and +0x0C arg table?
4. Can runtime PBR replacement key from selector +0x3C rows instead of shader pair alone?

Runtime probe fields added in psycho-graphics should be compared against this output:
  list +0x04 entry pointers, +0x08 count_low, +0x0C capacity, +0x0E grow_count, +0x10 active_count
  entry +0x00 resource, +0x04 row, +0x07 selector_flag, +0x09 arg_count, +0x0A arg_capacity, +0x0B layer, +0x0C args
